990	p76	L41	The Union institutions, bodies, offices or agencies and the governments of the Member States undertake to respect this principle and not to seek to influence the members of the decision-making bodies of the ECB or of the national central banks in the performance of their tasks.
991	p76	L47	Article 8 General principle The ESCB shall be governed by the decision-making bodies of the ECB.
992	p77	L4	Article 9 The European Central Bank 9.
993	p77	L6	The ECB which, in accordance with Article 282(3) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, shall have legal personality, shall enjoy in each of the Member States the most extensive legal capacity accorded to legal persons under its law; it may, in particular, acquire or dispose of movable and immovable property and may be a party to legal proceedings.
994	p77	L12	The ECB shall ensure that the tasks conferred upon the ESCB under Article 127(2), (3) and (5) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union are implemented either by its own activities pursuant to this Statute or through the national central banks pursuant to Articles 12.
995	p77	L14	1 and 14.
996	p77	L18	In accordance with Article 129(1) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the decision making bodies of the ECB shall be the Governing Council and the Executive Board.
997	p77	L22	Article 10 The Governing Council 10.
998	p77	L24	In accordance with Article 283(1) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the Governing Council shall comprise the members of the Executive Board of the ECB and the governors of the national central banks of the Member States whose currency is the euro.
999	p77	L29	10.
1000	p77	L29	Each member of the Governing Council shall have one vote.
1001	p77	L29	As from the date on which the number of members of the Governing Council exceeds 21, each member of the Executive Board shall have one vote and the number of governors with a voting right shall be 15.
1002	p77	L31	The latter voting rights shall be assigned and shall rotate as follows: — as from the date on which the number of governors exceeds 15, until it reaches 22, the governors shall be allocated to two groups, according to a ranking of the size of the share of their national central bank's Member State in the aggregate gross domestic product at market prices and in the total aggregated balance sheet of the monetary financial institutions of the Member States whose currency is the euro.
1003	p77	L39	The shares in the aggregate gross domestic product at market prices and in the total aggregated balance sheet of the monetary financial institutions shall be assigned weights of 5/6 and 1/6, respectively.
1004	p77	L41	The first group shall be composed of five governors and the second group of the remaining governors.
1005	p77	L42	The frequency of voting rights of the governors allocated to the first group shall not be lower than the frequency of voting rights of those of the second group.
1006	p77	L44	Subject to the previous sentence, the first group shall be assigned four voting rights and the second group eleven voting rights, — as from the date on which the number of governors reaches 22, the governors shall be allocated to three groups according to a ranking based on the above criteria.
1007	p77	L49	The first group shall be composed of five governors and shall be assigned four voting rights.
1008	p77	L50	The second group shall be composed of half of the total number of governors, with any fraction rounded up to the nearest integer, and shall be assigned eight voting rights.
1009	p77	L52	The third group shall be composed of the remaining governors and shall be assigned three voting rights, — within each group, the governors shall have their voting rights for equal amounts of time, — for the calculation of the shares in the aggregate gross domestic product at market prices Article 29.
1010	p78	L8	2 shall apply.
1011	p78	L8	The total aggregated balance sheet of the monetary financial institutions shall be calculated in accordance with the statistical framework applying in the Union at the time of the calculation, — whenever the aggregate gross domestic product at market prices is adjusted in accordance with Article 29.
1012	p78	L14	3, or whenever the number of governors increases, the size and/or composition of the groups shall be adjusted in accordance with the above principles, — the Governing Council, acting by a two-thirds majority of all its members, with and without a voting right, shall take all measures necessary for the implementation of the above principles and may decide to postpone the start of the rotation system until the date on which the number of governors exceeds 18.
1013	p78	L24	The right to vote shall be exercised in person.
1014	p78	L24	By way of derogation from this rule, the Rules of Procedure referred to in Article 12.
1015	p78	L25	3 may lay down that members of the Governing Council may cast their vote by means of teleconferencing.
1016	p78	L26	These rules shall also provide that a member of the Governing Council who is prevented from attending meetings of the Governing Council for a prolonged period may appoint an alternate as a member of the Governing Council.
1017	p78	L31	The provisions of the previous paragraphs are without prejudice to the voting rights of all members of the Governing Council, with and without a voting right, under Articles 10.
1018	p78	L32	3, 40.
1019	p78	L32	2 and 40.
1020	p78	L35	Save as otherwise provided for in this Statute, the Governing Council shall act by a simple majority of the members having a voting right.
1021	p78	L36	In the event of a tie, the President shall have the casting vote.
1022	p78	L39	In order for the Governing Council to vote, there shall be a quorum of two-thirds of the members having a voting right.
1023	p78	L40	If the quorum is not met, the President may convene an extraordinary meeting at which decisions may be taken without regard to the quorum.
1024	p78	L44	10.
1025	p78	L44	For any decisions to be taken under Articles 28, 29, 30, 32 and 33, the votes in the Governing Council shall be weighted according to the national central banks' shares in the subscribed capital of the ECB.
1026	p78	L46	The weights of the votes of the members of the Executive Board shall be zero.
1027	p78	L46	A decision requiring a qualified majority shall be adopted if the votes cast in favour represent at least two thirds of the subscribed capital of the ECB and represent at least half of the shareholders.
1028	p78	L48	If a Governor is unable to be present, he may nominate an alternate to cast his weighted vote.
1029	p78	L52	10.
1030	p78	L52	The proceedings of the meetings shall be confidential.
1031	p78	L52	The Governing Council may decide to make the outcome of its deliberations public.
1032	p78	L56	10.
1033	p78	L56	The Governing Council shall meet at least 10 times a year.
1034	p79	L4	Article 11 The Executive Board 11.
1035	p79	L6	In accordance with the first subparagraph of Article 283(2) of the Treaty on the Func­ tioning of the European Union, the Executive Board shall comprise the President, the Vice-President and four other members.
1036	p79	L11	The members shall perform their duties on a full-time basis.
1037	p79	L11	No member shall engage in any occupation, whether gainful or not, unless exemption is exceptionally granted by the Governing Council.
1038	p79	L16	11.
1039	p79	L16	In accordance with the second subparagraph of Article 283(2) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the President, the Vice-President and the other members of the Executive Board shall be appointed by the European Council, acting by a qualified majority, from among persons of recognised standing and professional experience in monetary or banking matters, on a recommendation from the Council after it has consulted the European Parliament and the Governing Council.
1040	p79	L24	Their term of office shall be eight years and shall not be renewable.
1041	p79	L27	Only nationals of Member States may be members of the Executive Board.
1042	p79	L30	11.
1043	p79	L30	The terms and conditions of employment of the members of the Executive Board, in particular their salaries, pensions and other social security benefits shall be the subject of contracts with the ECB and shall be fixed by the Governing Council on a proposal from a Committee comprising three members appointed by the Governing Council and three members appointed by the Council.
1044	p79	L34	The members of the Executive Board shall not have the right to vote on matters referred to in this paragraph.
1045	p79	L38	11.
1046	p79	L38	If a member of the Executive Board no longer fulfils the conditions required for the performance of his duties or if he has been guilty of serious misconduct, the Court of Justice may, on application by the Governing Council or the Executive Board, compulsorily retire him.
1047	p79	L43	11.
1048	p79	L43	Each member of the Executive Board present in person shall have the right to vote and shall have, for that purpose, one vote.
1049	p79	L44	Save as otherwise provided, the Executive Board shall act by a simple majority of the votes cast.
1050	p79	L45	In the event of a tie, the President shall have the casting vote.
1051	p79	L45	The voting arrangements shall be specified in the Rules of Procedure referred to in Article 12.
1052	p79	L49	11.
1053	p79	L49	The Executive Board shall be responsible for the current business of the ECB.
1054	p79	L52	11.
1055	p79	L52	Any vacancy on the Executive Board shall be filled by the appointment of a new member in accordance with Article 11.
1056	p80	L4	Article 12 Responsibilities of the decision-making bodies 12.
1057	p80	L6	The Governing Council shall adopt the guidelines and take the decisions necessary to ensure the performance of the tasks entrusted to the ESCB under these Treaties and this Statute.
1058	p80	L7	The Governing Council shall formulate the monetary policy of the Union including, as appropriate, decisions relating to intermediate monetary objectives, key interest rates and the supply of reserves in the ESCB, and shall establish the necessary guidelines for their implementation.
1059	p80	L12	The Executive Board shall implement monetary policy in accordance with the guidelines and decisions laid down by the Governing Council.
1060	p80	L13	In doing so the Executive Board shall give the necessary instructions to national central banks.
1061	p80	L14	In addition the Executive Board may have certain powers delegated to it where the Governing Council so decides.
1062	p80	L17	To the extent deemed possible and appropriate and without prejudice to the provisions of this Article, the ECB shall have recourse to the national central banks to carry out operations which form part of the tasks of the ESCB.
1063	p80	L21	12.
1064	p80	L21	The Executive Board shall have responsibility for the preparation of meetings of the Governing Council.
1065	p80	L24	12.
1066	p80	L24	The Governing Council shall adopt Rules of Procedure which determine the internal organ­ isation of the ECB and its decision-making bodies.
1067	p80	L27	12.
1068	p80	L27	The Governing Council shall exercise the advisory functions referred to in Article 4.
1069	p80	L29	12.
1070	p80	L29	The Governing Council shall take the decisions referred to in Article 6.
1071	p80	L31	Article 13 The President 13.
1072	p80	L33	The President or, in his absence, the Vice-President shall chair the Governing Council and the Executive Board of the ECB.
1073	p80	L36	13.
1074	p80	L36	Without prejudice to Article 38, the President or his nominee shall represent the ECB externally.
1075	p80	L39	Article 14 National central banks 14.
1076	p80	L41	In accordance with Article 131 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, each Member State shall ensure that its national legislation, including the statutes of its national central bank, is compatible with these Treaties and this Statute.
1077	p80	L45	14.
1078	p80	L45	The statutes of the national central banks shall, in particular, provide that the term of office of a Governor of a national central bank shall be no less than five years.
1079	p81	L4	A Governor may be relieved from office only if he no longer fulfils the conditions required for the performance of his duties or if he has been guilty of serious misconduct.
1080	p81	L5	A decision to this effect may be referred to the Court of Justice by the Governor concerned or the Governing Council on grounds of infringement of these Treaties or of any rule of law relating to their application.
1081	p81	L7	Such proceedings shall be instituted within two months of the publication of the decision or of its notification to the plaintiff or, in the absence thereof, of the day on which it came to the knowledge of the latter, as the case may be.
1082	p81	L13	14.
1083	p81	L13	The national central banks are an integral part of the ESCB and shall act in accordance with the guidelines and instructions of the ECB.
1084	p81	L14	The Governing Council shall take the necessary steps to ensure compliance with the guidelines and instructions of the ECB, and shall require that any necessary information be given to it.
1085	p81	L19	14.
1086	p81	L19	National central banks may perform functions other than those specified in this Statute unless the Governing Council finds, by a majority of two thirds of the votes cast, that these interfere with the objectives and tasks of the ESCB.
1087	p81	L21	Such functions shall be performed on the responsibility and liability of national central banks and shall not be regarded as being part of the functions of the ESCB.
1088	p81	L26	Article 15 Reporting commitments 15.
1089	p81	L28	The ECB shall draw up and publish reports on the activities of the ESCB at least quarterly.
1090	p81	L31	15.
1091	p81	L31	A consolidated financial statement of the ESCB shall be published each week.
1092	p81	L34	15.
1093	p81	L34	In accordance with Article 284(3) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the ECB shall address an annual report on the activities of the ESCB and on the monetary policy of both the previous and the current year to the European Parliament, the Council and the Commission, and also to the European Council.
1094	p81	L40	15.
1095	p81	L40	The reports and statements referred to in this Article shall be made available to interested parties free of charge.
1096	p81	L44	Article 16 Banknotes In accordance with Article 128(1) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the Governing Council shall have the exclusive right to authorise the issue of euro banknotes within the Union.
1097	p81	L48	The ECB and the national central banks may issue such notes.
1098	p81	L48	The banknotes issued by the ECB and the national central banks shall be the only such notes to have the status of legal tender within the Union.
1099	p81	L53	The ECB shall respect as far as possible existing practices regarding the issue and design of bank­ notes.
1100	p82	L3	CHAPTER IV MONETARY FUNCTIONS AND OPERATIONS OF THE ESCB Article 17 Accounts with the ECB and the national central banks In order to conduct their operations, the ECB and the national central banks may open accounts for credit institutions, public entities and other market participants and accept assets, including book entry securities, as collateral.
1101	p82	L14	Article 18 Open market and credit operations 18.
1102	p82	L16	In order to achieve the objectives of the ESCB and to carry out its tasks, the ECB and the national central banks may: — operate in the financial markets by buying and selling outright (spot and forward) or under repurchase agreement and by lending or borrowing claims and marketable instruments, whether in euro or other currencies, as well as precious metals; — conduct credit operations with credit institutions and other market participants, with lending being based on adequate collateral.
1103	p82	L32	18.
1104	p82	L32	The ECB shall establish general principles for open market and credit operations carried out by itself or the national central banks, including for the announcement of conditions under which they stand ready to enter into such transactions.
1105	p82	L38	Article 19 Minimum reserves 19.
1106	p82	L40	Subject to Article 2, the ECB may require credit institutions established in Member States to hold minimum reserve on accounts with the ECB and national central banks in pursuance of monetary policy objectives.
1107	p82	L42	Regulations concerning the calculation and determination of the required minimum reserves may be established by the Governing Council.
1108	p82	L43	In cases of non- compliance the ECB shall be entitled to levy penalty interest and to impose other sanctions with comparable effect.
1109	p82	L49	19.
1110	p82	L49	For the application of this Article, the Council shall, in accordance with the procedure laid down in Article 41, define the basis for minimum reserves and the maximum permissible ratios between those reserves and their basis, as well as the appropriate sanctions in cases of non- compliance.
1111	p83	L4	Article 20 Other instruments of monetary control The Governing Council may, by a majority of two thirds of the votes cast, decide upon the use of such other operational methods of monetary control as it sees fit, respecting Article 2.
1112	p83	L10	The Council shall, in accordance with the procedure laid down in Article 41, define the scope of such methods if they impose obligations on third parties.
1113	p83	L14	Article 21 Operations with public entities 21.
1114	p83	L16	In accordance with Article 123 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, overdrafts or any other type of credit facility with the ECB or with the national central banks in favour of Union institutions, bodies, offices or agencies, central governments, regional, local or other public authorities, other bodies governed by public law, or public undertakings of Member States shall be prohibited, as shall the purchase directly from them by the ECB or national central banks of debt instruments.
1115	p83	L24	21.
1116	p83	L24	The ECB and national central banks may act as fiscal agents for the entities referred to in Article 21.
1117	p83	L28	21.
1118	p83	L28	The provisions of this Article shall not apply to publicly owned credit institutions which, in the context of the supply of reserves by central banks, shall be given the same treatment by national central banks and the ECB as private credit institutions.
1119	p83	L33	Article 22 Clearing and payment systems The ECB and national central banks may provide facilities, and the ECB may make regulations, to ensure efficient and sound clearing and payment systems within the Union and with other countries.
1120	p83	L39	Article 23 External operations The ECB and national central banks may: — establish relations with central banks and financial institutions in other countries and, where appropriate, with international organisations; — acquire and sell spot and forward all types of foreign exchange assets and precious metals; the term "foreign exchange asset" shall include securities and all other assets in the currency of any country or units of account and in whatever form held; — hold and manage the assets referred to in this Article; — conduct all types of banking transactions in relations with third countries and international organisations, including borrowing and lending operations.
1121	p84	L11	Article 24 Other operations In addition to operations arising from their tasks, the ECB and national central banks may enter into operations for their administrative purposes or for their staff.
1122	p84	L17	CHAPTER V PRUDENTIAL SUPERVISION Article 25 Prudential supervision 25.
1123	p84	L22	The ECB may offer advice to and be consulted by the Council, the Commission and the competent authorities of the Member States on the scope and implementation of Union legislation relating to the prudential supervision of credit institutions and to the stability of the financial system.
1124	p84	L27	25.
1125	p84	L27	In accordance with any regulation of the Council under Article 127(6) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the ECB may perform specific tasks concerning policies relating to the prudential supervision of credit institutions and other financial institutions with the exception of insurance undertakings.
1126	p84	L33	CHAPTER VI FINANCIAL PROVISIONS OF THE ESCB Article 26 Financial accounts 26.
1127	p84	L38	The financial year of the ECB and national central banks shall begin on the first day of January and end on the last day of December.
1128	p84	L42	26.
1129	p84	L42	The annual accounts of the ECB shall be drawn up by the Executive Board, in accordance with the principles established by the Governing Council.
1130	p84	L43	The accounts shall be approved by the Governing Council and shall thereafter be published.
1131	p84	L47	26.
1132	p84	L47	For analytical and operational purposes, the Executive Board shall draw up a consolidated balance sheet of the ESCB, comprising those assets and liabilities of the national central banks that fall within the ESCB.
1133	p85	L4	26.
1134	p85	L4	For the application of this Article, the Governing Council shall establish the necessary rules for standardising the accounting and reporting of operations undertaken by the national central banks.
1135	p85	L10	Article 27 Auditing 27.
1136	p85	L12	The accounts of the ECB and national central banks shall be audited by independent external auditors recommended by the Governing Council and approved by the Council.
1137	p85	L13	The auditors shall have full power to examine all books and accounts of the ECB and national central banks and obtain full information about their transactions.
1138	p85	L19	27.
1139	p85	L19	The provisions of Article 287 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union shall only apply to an examination of the operational efficiency of the management of the ECB.
1140	p85	L24	Article 28 Capital of the ECB 28.
1141	p85	L26	The capital of the ECB shall be euro 5 000 million.
1142	p85	L26	The capital may be increased by such amounts as may be decided by the Governing Council acting by the qualified majority provided for in Article 10.
1143	p85	L28	3, within the limits and under the conditions set by the Council under the procedure laid down in Article 41.
1144	p85	L33	28.
1145	p85	L33	The national central banks shall be the sole subscribers to and holders of the capital of the ECB.
1146	p85	L34	The subscription of capital shall be according to the key established in accordance with Article 29.
1147	p85	L39	28.
1148	p85	L39	The Governing Council, acting by the qualified majority provided for in Article 10.
1149	p85	L39	3, shall determine the extent to which and the form in which the capital shall be paid up.
1150	p85	L44	28.
1151	p85	L44	Subject to Article 28.
1152	p85	L44	5, the shares of the national central banks in the subscribed capital of the ECB may not be transferred, pledged or attached.
1153	p85	L49	28.
1154	p85	L49	If the key referred to in Article 29 is adjusted, the national central banks shall transfer among themselves capital shares to the extent necessary to ensure that the distribution of capital shares corresponds to the adjusted key.
1155	p85	L51	The Governing Council shall determine the terms and conditions of such transfers.
1156	p86	L4	Article 29 Key for capital subscription 29.
1157	p86	L6	The key for subscription of the ECB's capital, fixed for the first time in 1998 when the ESCB was established, shall be determined by assigning to each national central bank a weighting in this key equal to the sum of: — 50 % of the share of its respective Member State in the population of the Union in the penultimate year preceding the establishment of the ESCB; — 50 % of the share of its respective Member State in the gross domestic product at market prices of the Union as recorded in the last five years preceding the penultimate year before the establishment of the ESCB.
1158	p86	L17	The percentages shall be rounded up or down to the nearest multiple of 0,0001 percentage points.
1159	p86	L19	29.
1160	p86	L19	The statistical data to be used for the application of this Article shall be provided by the Commission in accordance with the rules adopted by the Council under the procedure provided for in Article 41.
1161	p86	L23	29.
1162	p86	L23	The weightings assigned to the national central banks shall be adjusted every five years after the establishment of the ESCB by analogy with the provisions laid down in Article 29.
1163	p86	L24	The adjusted key shall apply with effect from the first day of the following year.
1164	p86	L27	29.
1165	p86	L27	The Governing Council shall take all other measures necessary for the application of this Article.
1166	p86	L30	Article 30 Transfer of foreign reserve assets to the ECB 30.
1167	p86	L32	Without prejudice to Article 28, the ECB shall be provided by the national central banks with foreign reserve assets, other than Member States' currencies, euro, IMF reserve positions and SDRs, up to an amount equivalent to euro 50 000 million.
1168	p86	L34	The Governing Council shall decide upon the proportion to be called up by the ECB following its establishment and the amounts called up at later dates.
1169	p86	L36	The ECB shall have the full right to hold and manage the foreign reserves that are transferred to it and to use them for the purposes set out in this Statute.
1170	p86	L39	30.
1171	p86	L39	The contributions of each national central bank shall be fixed in proportion to its share in the subscribed capital of the ECB.
1172	p86	L42	30.
1173	p86	L42	Each national central bank shall be credited by the ECB with a claim equivalent to its contribution.
1174	p86	L43	The Governing Council shall determine the denomination and remuneration of such claims.
1175	p86	L46	30.
1176	p86	L46	Further calls of foreign reserve assets beyond the limit set in Article 30.
1177	p86	L46	1 may be effected by the ECB, in accordance with Article 30.
1178	p86	L47	2, within the limits and under the conditions set by the Council in accordance with the procedure laid down in Article 41.
1179	p87	L4	30.
1180	p87	L4	The ECB may hold and manage IMF reserve positions and SDRs and provide for the pooling of such assets.
1181	p87	L7	30.
1182	p87	L7	The Governing Council shall take all other measures necessary for the application of this Article.
1183	p87	L10	Article 31 Foreign reserve assets held by national central banks 31.
1184	p87	L12	The national central banks shall be allowed to perform transactions in fulfilment of their obligations towards international organisations in accordance with Article 23.
1185	p87	L15	31.
1186	p87	L15	All other operations in foreign reserve assets remaining with the national central banks after the transfers referred to in Article 30, and Member States' transactions with their foreign exchange working balances shall, above a certain limit to be established within the framework of Article 31.
1187	p87	L17	3, be subject to approval by the ECB in order to ensure consistency with the exchange rate and monetary policies of the Union.
1188	p87	L21	31.
1189	p87	L21	The Governing Council shall issue guidelines with a view to facilitating such operations.
1190	p87	L23	Article 32 Allocation of monetary income of national central banks 32.
1191	p87	L25	The income accruing to the national central banks in the performance of the ESCB's monetary policy function (hereinafter referred to as "monetary income") shall be allocated at the end of each financial year in accordance with the provisions of this Article.
1192	p87	L29	32.
1193	p87	L29	The amount of each national central bank's monetary income shall be equal to its annual income derived from its assets held against notes in circulation and deposit liabilities to credit institutions.
1194	p87	L31	These assets shall be earmarked by national central banks in accordance with guidelines to be established by the Governing Council.
1195	p87	L34	32.
1196	p87	L34	If, after the introduction of the euro, the balance sheet structures of the national central banks do not, in the judgment of the Governing Council, permit the application of Article 32.
1197	p87	L35	2, the Governing Council, acting by a qualified majority, may decide that, by way of derogation from Article 32.
1198	p87	L37	2, monetary income shall be measured according to an alternative method for a period of not more than five years.
1199	p87	L40	32.
1200	p87	L40	The amount of each national central bank's monetary income shall be reduced by an amount equivalent to any interest paid by that central bank on its deposit liabilities to credit institutions in accordance with Article 19.
1201	p87	L44	The Governing Council may decide that national central banks shall be indemnified against costs incurred in connection with the issue of banknotes or in exceptional circumstances for specific losses arising from monetary policy operations undertaken for the ESCB.
1202	p87	L46	Indemnification shall be in a form deemed appropriate in the judgment of the Governing Council; these amounts may be offset against the national central banks' monetary income.
1203	p88	L4	32.
1204	p88	L4	The sum of the national central banks' monetary income shall be allocated to the national central banks in proportion to their paid up shares in the capital of the ECB, subject to any decision taken by the Governing Council pursuant to Article 33.
1205	p88	L8	32.
1206	p88	L8	The clearing and settlement of the balances arising from the allocation of monetary income shall be carried out by the ECB in accordance with guidelines established by the Governing Council.
1207	p88	L11	32.
1208	p88	L11	The Governing Council shall take all other measures necessary for the application of this Article.
1209	p88	L14	Article 33 Allocation of net profits and losses of the ECB 33.
1210	p88	L16	The net profit of the ECB shall be transferred in the following order: (a) an amount to be determined by the Governing Council, which may not exceed 20 % of the net profit, shall be transferred to the general reserve fund subject to a limit equal to 100 % of the capital; (b) the remaining net profit shall be distributed to the shareholders of the ECB in proportion to their paid-up shares.
1211	p88	L25	33.
1212	p88	L25	In the event of a loss incurred by the ECB, the shortfall may be offset against the general reserve fund of the ECB and, if necessary, following a decision by the Governing Council, against the monetary income of the relevant financial year in proportion and up to the amounts allocated to the national central banks in accordance with Article 32.
1213	p88	L30	CHAPTER VII GENERAL PROVISIONS Article 34 Legal acts 34.
1214	p88	L35	In accordance with Article 132 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the ECB shall: — make regulations to the extent necessary to implement the tasks defined in Article 3.
1215	p88	L38	1, first indent, Articles 19.
1216	p88	L39	1, 22 or 25.
1217	p88	L39	2 and in cases which shall be laid down in the acts of the Council referred to in Article 41; — take decisions necessary for carrying out the tasks entrusted to the ESCB under these Treaties and this Statute; — make recommendations and deliver opinions.
1218	p88	L47	34.
1219	p88	L47	The ECB may decide to publish its decisions, recommendations and opinions.
1220	p89	L4	34.
1221	p89	L4	Within the limits and under the conditions adopted by the Council under the procedure laid down in Article 41, the ECB shall be entitled to impose fines or periodic penalty payments on undertakings for failure to comply with obligations under its regulations and decisions.
1222	p89	L9	Article 35 Judicial control and related matters 35.
1223	p89	L11	The acts or omissions of the ECB shall be open to review or interpretation by the Court of Justice of the European Union in the cases and under the conditions laid down in the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union.
1224	p89	L13	The ECB may institute proceedings in the cases and under the conditions laid down in the Treaties.
1225	p89	L17	35.
1226	p89	L17	Disputes between the ECB, on the one hand, and its creditors, debtors or any other person, on the other, shall be decided by the competent national courts, save where jurisdiction has been conferred upon the Court of Justice of the European Union.
1227	p89	L22	35.
1228	p89	L22	The ECB shall be subject to the liability regime provided for in Article 340 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union.
1229	p89	L23	The national central banks shall be liable according to their respective national laws.
1230	p89	L27	35.
1231	p89	L27	The Court of Justice of the European Union shall have jurisdiction to give judgment pursuant to any arbitration clause contained in a contract concluded by or on behalf of the ECB, whether that contract be governed by public or private law.
1232	p89	L32	35.
1233	p89	L32	A decision of the ECB to bring an action before the Court of Justice of the European Union shall be taken by the Governing Council.
1234	p89	L36	35.
1235	p89	L36	The Court of Justice of the European Union shall have jurisdiction in disputes concerning the fulfilment by a national central bank of obligations under the Treaties and this Statute.
1236	p89	L37	If the ECB considers that a national central bank has failed to fulfil an obligation under the Treaties and this Statute, it shall deliver a reasoned opinion on the matter after giving the national central bank concerned the opportunity to submit its observations.
1237	p89	L40	If the national central bank concerned does not comply with the opinion within the period laid down by the ECB, the latter may bring the matter before the Court of Justice of the European Union.
1238	p89	L45	Article 36 Staff 36.
1239	p89	L47	The Governing Council, on a proposal from the Executive Board, shall lay down the conditions of employment of the staff of the ECB.
1240	p89	L51	36.
1241	p89	L51	The Court of Justice of the European Union shall have jurisdiction in any dispute between the ECB and its servants within the limits and under the conditions laid down in the conditions of employment.
1242	p90	L4	Article 37 (ex Article 38) Professional secrecy 37.
1243	p90	L6	Members of the governing bodies and the staff of the ECB and the national central banks shall be required, even after their duties have ceased, not to disclose information of the kind covered by the obligation of professional secrecy.
1244	p90	L12	37.
1245	p90	L12	Persons having access to data covered by Union legislation imposing an obligation of secrecy shall be subject to such legislation.
1246	p90	L17	Article 38 (ex Article 39) Signatories The ECB shall be legally committed to third parties by the President or by two members of the Executive Board or by the signatures of two members of the staff of the ECB who have been duly authorised by the President to sign on behalf of the ECB.
1247	p90	L25	Article 39 (ex Article 40) Privileges and immunities The ECB shall enjoy in the territories of the Member States such privileges and immunities as are necessary for the performance of its tasks, under the conditions laid down in the Protocol on the privileges and immunities of the European Union.

1330	p93	L35	Article 48 (ex Article 49) Deferred payment of capital, reserves and provisions of the ECB 48.
1331	p93	L37	The central bank of a Member State whose derogation has been abrogated shall pay up its subscribed share of the capital of the ECB to the same extent as the central banks of other Member States whose currency is the euro, and shall transfer to the ECB foreign reserve assets in accordance with Article 30.
1332	p93	L40	The sum to be transferred shall be determined by multiplying the euro value at current exchange rates of the foreign reserve assets which have already been transferred to the ECB in accordance with Article 30.
1333	p93	L42	1, by the ratio between the number of shares subscribed by the national central bank concerned and the number of shares already paid up by the other national central banks.
1334	p93	L46	48.
1335	p93	L46	In addition to the payment to be made in accordance with Article 48.
1336	p93	L46	1, the central bank concerned shall contribute to the reserves of the ECB, to those provisions equivalent to reserves, and to the amount still to be appropriated to the reserves and provisions corresponding to the balance of the profit and loss account as at 31 December of the year prior to the abrogation of the derogation.
1337	p94	L4	The sum to be contributed shall be determined by multiplying the amount of the reserves, as defined above and as stated in the approved balance sheet of the ECB, by the ratio between the number of shares subscribed by the central bank concerned and the number of shares already paid up by the other central banks.
1338	p94	L9	48.
1339	p94	L9	Upon one or more countries becoming Member States and their respective national central banks becoming part of the ESCB, the subscribed capital of the ECB and the limit on the amount of foreign reserve assets that may be transferred to the ECB shall be automatically increased.
1340	p94	L11	The increase shall be determined by multiplying the respective amounts then prevailing by the ratio, within the expanded capital key, between the weighting of the entering national central banks concerned and the weighting of the national central banks already members of the ESCB.
1341	p94	L14	Each national central bank's weighting in the capital key shall be calculated by analogy with Article 29.
1342	p94	L15	1 and in compliance with Article 29.
